### [254] [Rethinking Vacuity for OOD Detection in Evidential Deep Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06382)
*Claire McNamara*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文实证和理论证明了在证据深度学习（EDL）中，基于不确定性质量（vacuity/UM）的OOD检测对类别基数（K）的差异高度敏感。当ID和OOD的类别数不一致时，AUROC和AUPR会被人为膨胀，偏差可达0.3-0.6以上。论文进一步讨论了因果语言模型在多项选择问答（MCQA）情境下的评估问题，呼吁更清晰的ID/OOD定义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有EDL中使用不确定性质量（UM = K/S）作为OOD检测指标时，类别数K和信念强度S之间在现实中不存在线性关系（因为EDL会抑制错误类别的证据）。当ID和OOD的类别基数K不一致时，UM指标会产生系统性偏差，导致AUROC/AUPR被虚假提升。作者意在揭示这一评估伪影并论证问题的严重性。

Method: 通过实验对比标准EDL和IB-EDL在ID与OOD类别基数相差1时的AUROC/AUPR差异；结合理论分析说明UM公式中K/S的非线性关系导致评估偏差；进一步将讨论延伸至基于EDL微调的大语言模型在MCQA任务中的OOD评估问题。

Result: 当ID和OOD的类别数仅差1时：标准EDL的AUROC偏差可达0.318，AUPR偏差达0.613；IB-EDL的AUROC偏差达0.360，AUPR偏差达0.683。这表明UM-based OOD检测结果可以被人为操控，而与模型预测质量无关。

Conclusion: EDL中基于vacuity的OOD检测对类别基数差异极度敏感，研究者在使用该指标时必须确保ID和OOD的类别数严格一致，否则会导致误导性结论。同时，在LLM的MCQA场景中需要更规范的ID/OOD定义。

Abstract: Vacuity, or Uncertainty Mass (UM), is commonly used as a metric to evaluate Out-of-Distribution (OOD) detection in Evidential Deep Learning (EDL). It generally involves dividing the number of classes ($K$) by the total strength of belief ($S$) of the model's predictions, where $S$ is derived from summing the Dirichlet parameters. As such, UM is sensitive to the cardinality of $K$. In particular, it is unlikely in practice that there is a linear relationship between $K$ and $S$ as $K$ and $S$ increase due to the nature of EDL (suppressing incorrectly assigned evidence). As a result, when comparing In Distribution (ID) and OOD results, it is important that $K_{\mathrm{ID}}$ and $K_{\mathrm{OOD}}$ are equal; something that is not always ensured in practice. We provide an empirical demonstration of how results for AUROC and AUPR can substantially differ when class cardinality between ID and OOD differs by 1, with AUROC differing by as much as 0.318 and AUPR by 0.613 for standard EDL, and AUROC by 0.360 and AUPR by 0.683 for IB-EDL. More concretely, our findings isolate an evaluation artefact: when K differs between ID and OOD, AUROC/AUPR can be artificially inflated without any change in model predictions. We further discuss the evaluation of EDL over causal language models using Multiple-Choice Question-Answer (MCQA) datasets and argue for clearer definitions of ID and OOD in this context. Our primary contribution is an empirical and theoretical demonstration that vacuity-based OOD detection in EDL-fine-tuned LLMs is highly sensitive to uncontrolled differences in evaluated class cardinality.

</details>


### [255] [Knowledge Graphs, the Missing Link in Agentic AI-based Formal Verification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06434)
*Vaisakh Naduvodi Viswambharan,Keerthan Kopparam Radhakrishna,Deepak Narayan Gadde,Aman Kumar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于知识图谱的多智能体工作流，通过从规范、RTL和形式化工具反馈中提取结构化中间表示来生成SystemVerilog断言，并利用语法修复、反例引导和覆盖驱动三个优化循环提升断言质量，在七个基准设计中实现了78.5%-99.4%的形式化覆盖率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM生成SVA的方法将规范和RTL视为松散文本，导致规范与RTL之间缺乏有效关联，产生语义不匹配和频繁的语法错误，亟需一种能建立设计层级、信号、假设与属性间可追溯关联的结构化方法。

Method: 构建基于结构化中间表示的知识图谱，将规范、RTL和形式化工具反馈（语法诊断、反例、覆盖报告）中的需求、设计层级、信号、假设和属性链接起来；采用多智能体工作流查询和更新知识图谱，并驱动三个优化循环：语法修复循环（利用工具诊断）、反例引导修正循环（利用跟踪链接）、覆盖驱动属性增强循环。

Result: 在七个基准设计上，该方法持续生成可编译的SVA，语法修复开销低；形式化覆盖率达到78.5%-99.4%，但收敛性存在设计依赖性，复杂时序和算术推理仍具挑战。

Conclusion: 基于知识图谱的结构化上下文检索能有效改善规范到RTL的关联，提升断言合成质量，但当前LLM在处理复杂时序和算术逻辑时能力仍然有限。

Abstract: Recent advances in Large Language Models (LLMs) have enabled workflows that generate SystemVerilog Assertions (SVAs) from natural-language specifications, with the potential to accelerate Formal Verification (FV). However, high-quality assertion synthesis remains challenging because specifications are often ambiguous or incomplete and critical micro-architectural details reside in the Register Transfer Level (RTL). Many existing approaches treat the specification and RTL as loosely structured text, which weakens specification-to-RTL grounding and leads to semantic mismatches and frequent syntax failures during formal parsing and elaboration. This work addresses these limitations with a verification-centric Knowledge Graph (KG) constructed from structured Intermediate Representations (IRs) extracted from the specification, RTL, and formal-tool feedback, including syntax diagnostics, Counterexamples (CEXs), and coverage reports. The KG links requirements, design hierarchy, signals, assumptions, and properties to provide traceable, design-grounded context for generation. A multi-agent workflow queries and updates this KG to generate SVAs and to drive three refinement loops: syntax repair guided by tool diagnostics, CEX-guided correction using trace links, and coverage-directed property augmentation. Evaluation across seven benchmark designs indicates that KG-based context retrieval improves specification-to-RTL grounding and consistently produces compilable SVAs with low syntax-repair overhead. The approach achieves formal coverage ranging from 78.5% to 99.4%, though convergence exhibits design dependence with complex temporal and arithmetic reasoning remaining challenging for current LLM capabilities.

</details>


### [256] [SCRuB: Social Concept Reasoning under Rubric-Based Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06444)
*Jamelle Watson-Daniels,Himaghna Bhattacharjee,Skyler Wang,Brandon Handoko,Antonio Li,Anaelia Ovalle,Mahesh Pasupuleti,Candace Ross,Vidya Sarma,Arjun Subramonian,Karen Ullrich,Will van der Vaart,Yijing Xin,Maximilian Nickel*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 本研究首次提供了基于专家验证的社会概念推理评估饱和的证据：单轮考试式格式已达到模型和人类的表现天花板。这提示需要开发更复杂、多轮交互或多模态的评估范式来进一步推动该领域发展。

Abstract: While many studies of Large Language Model (LLM) reasoning capabilities emphasize mathematical or technical tasks, few address reasoning about social concepts: the abstract ideas shaping social norms, culture, and institutions. This understudied capability is essential for modern models acting as social agents, yet no systematic evaluation methodology targets it. We introduce SCRuB (Social Concept Reasoning under Rubric-Based Evaluation), a framework designed for this setting of task indeterminacy. Our goal is to measure the degree to which a model reasons about social concepts with the depth and critical rigor of a human expert. SCRuB proceeds in three phases: prompt construction from established sources, response generation by experts and models, and comparative evaluation using a five-dimensional critical thinking rubric. To enable generalization of the pipeline, we introduce a Panel of Disciplinary Perspectives ensemble validated against independent expert judges. We release SCRuBEval (n=4,711 evaluation prompts) and SCRuBAnnotations (300 expert-authored responses and 150 expert comparative judgments from 45 PhD-level scholars). Our results show that frontier models consistently outperform human experts across all five rubric dimensions. Across 1,170 pairwise comparisons, expert judges ranked a model response first in 80.8% of judgments and preferred model responses overall 74.4% of the time. Ultimately, this study provides the first expert-grounded demonstration of evaluation saturation for social concept reasoning: the single-turn exam-style format has reached its ceiling for models and humans alike.

### [257] [PrefixGuard: From LLM-Agent Traces to Online Failure-Warning Monitors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06455)
*Xinmiao Huang,Jinwei Hu,Rajarshi Roy,Changshun Wu,Yi Dong,Xiaowei Huang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: PrefixGuard提出了一种离线-在线结合的框架，通过StepView归纳步骤从原始trace中提取确定性的类型化步骤适配器，并训练监督式前缀风险评分器，实现轻量级在线预警。在多个基准上AUPRC达0.900/0.710/0.533/0.557，相比纯文本基线平均提升+0.137 AUPRC，同时揭示了可观测性上限和部署实用性的关键差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM智能体执行长序列工具调用任务时，最终结果检查往往滞后，无法及时干预。现有的在线预警方法要么依赖手工编写的事件模式（脆弱），要么在部署时使用LLM评判（成本高），缺乏轻量级、可泛化的前缀监控方案。

Method: 提出PrefixGuard框架，包含离线StepView归纳步骤（从原始trace样本中归纳确定性的类型化步骤适配器）和有监督的监控器训练（学习事件抽象和前缀风险评分器）。此外还提出了基于AUPRC的可观测性上界分析方法，以及后验的确定性有限自动机（DFA）提取方法用于有限状态审计。

Result: 在WebArena、τ²-Bench、SkillsBench和TerminalBench上，最强PrefixGuard监控器AUPRC分别达到0.900/0.710/0.533/0.557，相比纯文本基线平均提升+0.137 AUPRC。LLM评判在相同前缀预警协议下显著较弱。DFA在WebArena和τ²-Bench上保持紧凑（29和20状态），但在SkillsBench和TerminalBench上扩至151和187状态。首次警报诊断显示强排序不等同于部署实用性：WebArena排序良好但无法支持低误报警报。

Conclusion: PrefixGuard提供了一种实用的监控器合成配方，并给出了明确的可诊断性分析，用于判断前缀警告何时能转化为可操作的干预措施。该方法在多个基准上显著优于纯文本基线和LLM评判方案。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents now execute long, tool-using tasks where final outcome checks can arrive too late for intervention. Online warning requires lightweight prefix monitors over heterogeneous traces, but hand-authored event schemas are brittle and deployment-time LLM judging is costly. We introduce PrefixGuard, a trace-to-monitor framework with an offline StepView induction step followed by supervised monitor training. StepView induces deterministic typed-step adapters from raw trace samples, and the monitor learns an event abstraction and prefix-risk scorer from terminal outcomes. Across WebArena, $τ^2$-Bench, SkillsBench, and TerminalBench, the strongest PrefixGuard monitors reach 0.900/0.710/0.533/0.557 AUPRC. Using the strongest backend within each representation, they improve over raw-text controls by an average of +0.137 AUPRC. LLM judges remain substantially weaker under the same prefix-warning protocol. We also derive an observability ceiling on score-based area under the precision-recall curve (AUPRC) that separates monitor error from failures lacking evidence in the observed prefix. For finite-state audit, post-hoc deterministic finite automaton (DFA) extraction remains compact on WebArena and $τ^2$-Bench (29 and 20 states) but expands to 151 and 187 states on SkillsBench and TerminalBench. Finally, first-alert diagnostics show that strong ranking does not imply deployment utility: WebArena ranks well yet fails to support low-false-alarm alerts, whereas $τ^2$-Bench and TerminalBench retain more actionable early alerts. Together, these results position PrefixGuard as a practical monitor-synthesis recipe with explicit diagnostics for when prefix warnings translate into actionable interventions.

### [258] [Beyond Task Success: Measuring Workflow Fidelity in LLM-Based Agentic Payment Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06457)
*Donghao Huang,Joon Kiat Chua,Zhaoxia Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出Agentic Success Rate（ASR）指标，用于评估LLM多智能体系统的轨迹保真度。在支付场景HMASP中测试18个LLM和9万任务实例，发现ASR能识别出TSR和HF1无法发现的隐蔽问题（如跳过确认检查点），并通过ASR诊断指导的优化使某些模型TSR提升高达93.8个百分点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估指标（TSR和HF1）仅关注最终结果或无序路由决策，无法检测多智能体系统在执行过程中的轨迹偏离问题，尤其在支付等监管严格的领域，需要能够衡量执行序列保真度的细粒度指标。

Method: 提出ASR（Agentic Success Rate）指标，将性能分解为Transition Recall和Transition Precision，在转移级别比较观察到的和期望的智能体执行序列。在HMASP（分层多智能体支付系统）上对18个LLM进行9万个任务实例的评估。

Result: 18个模型中有10个在支付结账时系统性地跳过确认检查点（TSR和HF1无法检测），8个完美执行。GPT-4.1在TSR和HF1满分的情况下存在隐藏工作流捷径，GPT-5.2达到完美ASR。通过ASR诊断指导的优化，部分模型的TSR提升高达93.8个百分点。

Conclusion: 轨迹级别的评估在监管领域至关重要，ASR能够揭示传统指标无法发现的执行路径问题，且基于ASR的诊断可以有效指导系统优化，显著提升任务成功率。

Abstract: LLM-based multi-agent systems are increasingly deployed for payment workflows, yet prevailing metrics, Task Success Rate (TSR) and Agent Handoff F1-Score (HF1), capture only final outcomes or unordered routing decisions. We introduce the Agentic Success Rate (ASR), a trajectory-fidelity metric that compares observed and expected agent execution sequences at the transition level, decomposing performance into Transition Recall and Transition Precision. Applied to the Hierarchical Multi-Agent System for Payments (HMASP) across 18 LLMs and 90,000 task instances, ASR reveals that 10 of 18 models systematically skip a confirmation checkpoint during payment checkout, a deviation invisible to both TSR and HF1, while 8 models enforce the checkpoint perfectly. Notably, GPT-4.1 exhibits hidden workflow shortcuts despite achieving perfect TSR and HF1, while GPT-5.2 achieves perfect ASR. Prompt refinements and deterministic routing guards guided by ASR diagnostics yield substantial TSR improvements, with gains up to +93.8 percentage points for previously struggling models, demonstrating that trajectory-level evaluation is essential in regulated domains.

</details>


### [259] [ReasonSTL: Bridging Natural Language and Signal Temporal Logic via Tool-Augmented Process-Rewarded Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06483)
*Bowen Ye,Zhijian Li,Junyue Huang,Junkai Ma,Xiang Yin*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出ReasonSTL框架，将自然语言到STL的翻译过程分解为显式推理、确定性工具调用和结构化公式构建三个步骤，并引入过程奖励训练（process-rewarded training）来监督工具使用轨迹和最终公式，同时构建了基于真实世界信号的双语、计算感知基准STL-Bench。

Result: 使用ReasonSTL训练的4B模型在自动评估指标和人类评估中均达到最先进水平。

Abstract: Signal Temporal Logic (STL) is an expressive formal language for specifying spatio-temporal requirements over real-valued, real-time signals. It has been widely used for the verification and synthesis of autonomous systems and cyber-physical systems. In practice, however, users often express their requirements in natural language rather than in structured STL formulas, making natural-language-to-STL translation a critical yet challenging task. Manual specification requires temporal-logic expertise and cannot scale, while prompting commercial LLM APIs incurs substantial token costs and may expose sensitive system requirements to third-party services, raising privacy concerns for industrial deployment. To address these challenges, we present \textsc{ReasonSTL}, a tool-augmented framework that adapts local open-source language models for natural-language-to-STL generation. \textsc{ReasonSTL} decomposes the translation process into explicit reasoning, deterministic tool calls, and structured formula construction. We further introduce process-rewarded training to supervise both tool-use trajectories and final formulas, together with \textsc{STL-Bench}, a bilingual, computation-aware benchmark grounded in real-world signals. Experiments show that a 4B model trained with \textsc{ReasonSTL} achieves state-of-the-art performance in both automatic metrics and human evaluations, demonstrating that \textsc{ReasonSTL} provides a transparent, low-cost, and privacy-preserving alternative for formal specification drafting.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有SAE特征分析几乎完全依赖top-activating token列表或解码器权重向量，忽略了特征间共享的层次共现结构，缺乏对特征高阶结构关系的系统性考察。

Method: 将每个SAE特征建模为token共现图（节点为强激活附近高频token，边为局部上下文窗口内的共现关系）；采用自定义WL风格、频率分箱图核计算结构相似度；在GPT-2 Small的SAE特征上进行聚类分析。

Result: 图聚类恢复了启发式动机家族（标点模式、语言/脚本簇、代码模板），这些是解码器余弦相似度聚类无法恢复的；token直方图基线在整体纯度上更优，图视角提供互补性结构信息；聚类超参数和随机种子下稳定。

Conclusion: 图结构表示能揭示token频率和解码器权重视图单独无法捕获的结构关系，是现有特征分析方法的有效补充，而非替代。

Abstract: Sparse autoencoders (SAEs) have become central to mechanistic interpretability, decomposing transformer activations into monosemantic features. Yet existing analyses characterise features almost exclusively through top-activating token lists or decoder weight vectors, leaving the higher-order co-occurrence structure shared across features largely unexamined. We introduce a graph-structured representation in which each SAE feature is modelled as a token co-occurrence graph: nodes are the tokens most frequent near strong activations, and edges connect pairs that co-occur within local context windows. A custom WL-style, frequency-binned graph kernel then provides a similarity measure over this structural space. Applied as a proof of concept to features from a large SAE trained on GPT-2 Small and probed with a synthetic mixed-domain corpus, our clustering recovers heuristic motif families (punctuation-heavy patterns, language and script clusters, and code-like templates) that are not recovered by clustering on decoder cosine similarity. A token-histogram baseline achieves higher overall purity, so the contribution of the graph view is complementary rather than dominant: it surfaces structural relationships that token-frequency and decoder-weight views alone do not capture. Cluster assignments are stable across graph-construction hyperparameters and random seeds.

SpatialEpiBench includes 11 epidemic datasets with standardized rolling evaluations and outbreak-specific metrics. We evaluate adjacency-informed forecasting models with widely used epidemic priors that adapt general models to epidemiology, but find that most methods underperform a simple last-value baseline from 1 day to 1 month ahead, even during outbreaks and with these priors. We identify three major failure modes: (1) poor outbreak anticipation, (2) difficulty handling sparsity and noise, and (3) limited utility of common geographic adjacency for epidemiological spatial information. We release benchmark data, code, and instructions at https://github.com/Rachel-Lyu/SpatialEpiBench to support development of operationally useful epidemic forecasting models.

Abstract: We propose a deterministic adjoint matching framework that formulates human preference alignment for flow-based generative models as an optimal control problem over velocity fields. Building on this perspective, we introduce a truncated adjoint scheme that focuses computation on the terminal portion of the trajectory, where reward-relevant signals concentrate, which yields substantial computational savings while preserving alignment quality. We further generalize the framework beyond standard KL-based regularization, allowing more flexible trade-offs between alignment strength and distributional preservation. Experiments on SiT-XL/2 and FLUX.2-Klein-4B demonstrate consistent gains across multiple alignment metrics, along with substantially improved diversity and mode preservation.

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: NeuroAgent 是一个基于大语言模型的多智能体框架，能够自动化处理多模态神经影像数据（sMRI、fMRI、dMRI、PET）的预处理与分析流程。该框架采用层次化多智能体架构，配备反馈驱动的生成-执行-验证引擎，可在1,470名ADNI受试者数据上实现高达84.8%的端到端预处理正确率，并在四模态阿尔茨海默病分类中达到0.9518的AUC，显著减少人工干预。

Beyond preprocessing, downstream statistical analysis and disease classification commonly require task-specific code, evaluation protocols, and data-format conventions, creating additional barriers between raw acquisitions and reproducible scientific analysis. We present NeuroAgent, an LLM-driven agentic framework that automates key preprocessing and analysis steps for heterogeneous neuroimaging data, including sMRI, fMRI, dMRI, and PET, and supports interactive downstream analysis through natural-language queries. For Alzheimer's Disease classification using automatically preprocessed multimodal data, our agent ensemble achieves an AUC of 0.9518 with four modalities, outperforming all single-modality baselines. ### [265] [Discrete Elastic Ribbons: A Unified Discrete Differential Geometry Framework for One-Dimensional Energy Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05529)
*Shivam Kumar Panda,M Khalid Jawed*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出一个基于离散微分几何的统一框架，比较五种弹性带模型（Kirchhoff、Sadowsky、Wunderlich、Sano、Audoly）的弯曲-扭转耦合行为。通过预屈曲拱形结构的超临界叉形分岔基准测试，发现Sano模型与壳有限元模拟最吻合，且其计算开销与标准离散弹性杆（DER）相当。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于中心线的带状模型试图通过耦合弯曲-扭转能量来捕捉宽度依赖性，但由于缺乏统一的模拟框架，它们的相对准确性尚不明确。

Method: 基于离散微分几何构建统一框架，将能量表示为沿中心线的耦合弯曲-扭转应变度量函数（而非DER中二次弯曲能和扭转能的线性求和），推导解析梯度和Hessian矩阵以支持隐式时间积分。在该框架下系统比较五种带状模型，并以壳有限元模拟为基准。

Result: Sano模型在捕捉宽度依赖性分岔阈值方面与壳有限元模拟最接近；基于JAX的高性能实现达到O(N)每迭代计算成本，且Sano模型相比标准DER仅引入可忽略的额外开销。

Conclusion: 提出的统一框架有效评估了各带状模型的准确性，Sano模型在精度和计算效率之间取得了最佳平衡，为细长弹性带的数值模拟提供了可靠选择。

Abstract: Elastic ribbons, slender structures whose length ($L$), width ($W$), and thickness ($b$) satisfy $L \gg W \gg b$, exhibit mechanical behaviors intermediate between one-dimensional rods ($L \gg W, b$) and two-dimensional plates ($L, W \gg b$). In quadratic Kirchhoff-type rod-based frameworks, such as Discrete Elastic Rods (DER), the governing equilibrium equations are independent of width, and therefore these models cannot capture width-dependent mechanical effects. Reduced centerline-based ribbon models attempt to capture width dependence via coupled bending-twisting energies. However, their relative accuracy remain unclear due to the absence of a unified simulation framework. In this work, we formulate a framework grounded in discrete differential geometry where the energy is expressed as functions of coupled bending-twisting strain measures along the centerline, rather than a linear sum of quadratic bending and twisting energies in DER. We derive analytical gradients and Hessians of the energy that enable implicit time integration. Within this unified setting, we compare five ribbon models: Kirchhoff, Sadowsky, Wunderlich, Sano, and Audoly. As a benchmark, a straight ribbon is longitudinally constrained into a pre-buckled arch and subjected to transverse displacement, inducing a supercritical pitchfork bifurcation. Predicted bifurcation thresholds are compared against shell-based finite element simulations, with the Sano model providing the closest agreement in capturing width-dependent shifts. Our high-performance JAX-based implementation achieves $\mathcal{O}(N)$ per-iteration cost and also confirms that Sano model introduces negligible per-iteration overhead relative to standard DER.

</details>


### [266] [Marking strategies for adaptive mesh refinement: An efficiency-focused benchmark study for steady solid and fluid mechanics problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05234)
*Oliver Wege,Kaan Atak,Marek Behr,Norbert Hosters*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文系统比较了经典（最大值、Dörfler、分位数）与非经典（z-score、孤立森林）网格标记策略在自适应有限元分析中的性能，发现分位数和z-score标记最为稳健，Dörfler在大批量参数下有效，最大值标记对不规则场敏感，孤立森林在适当参数下可与经典方法媲美但激进设置时可能失败。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自适应网格细化（AMR）的效率不仅取决于细化本身，还高度依赖于标记单元进行细化的策略及其调优方式，但目前缺乏对不同标记策略的系统比较研究。

Method: 基于残差型Kelly误差估计器，驱动五种标记方法（最大值、Dörfler bulk-chasing、分位数、z-score、孤立森林），在稳态固体力学和流体力学问题上进行性能比较。

Result: 分位数和z-score标记最稳健；Dörfler在大批量参数下有效；最大值标记对不规则场敏感；孤立森林在宽松污染水平下可媲美经典方法，但激进设置下易失败。

Conclusion: 研究结果为选择平衡细化激进性与计算成本的自适应FEM标记策略提供了实用指导。

Abstract: Adaptive mesh refinement (AMR) is indispensable for efficient finite element analyses. However, its performance depends not only on the refinement itself but also on strategy to mark elements for refinement and the way it is tuned. This work compares classical marking methods (maximum, Dörfler bulk-chasing, quantile) with non-classical, statistically based approaches (z-score, Isolation Forest), all driven by the residual-based Kelly error estimator and tested on steady solid and fluid mechanics problems. The study finds quantile and z-score markings to be the most robust, Dörfler effective for large bulk parameters, and maximum marking sensitive to irregular fields. Isolation Forest can rival top classical methods with a generous contamination level but may fail under aggressive settings. These results offer practical guidance for selecting marking strategies that balance refinement aggressiveness and computational cost in adaptive FEM workflows.

</details>


### [267] [Scenario-driven optimization of passive vehicle suspensions: explaining the effectiveness of asymmetric damping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05235)
*José Geraldo Telles Ribeiro,Americo Cunha*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文通过场景驱动优化框架，系统论证了非对称阻尼在车辆悬架中的有效性，发现常见回弹-压缩阻尼比（2~3倍）并非普适常数，而是特定工况下的近优解。对称阻尼在中等激励下通常足够，非对称阻尼仅在严苛工况下必要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非对称阻尼（回弹阻尼通常为压缩阻尼的2~3倍）在车辆被动悬架中广泛应用，但该准则源于经验，缺乏基于车辆动力学和激励条件的系统性推导。现有文献未能解释其有效性背后的机理。

Method: 采用最小化四分之一车辆模型，将回弹和压缩阻尼比作为独立设计变量，利用随机交叉熵算法对非凸、基于仿真的目标函数进行优化，使用ISO 8608标准路面激励，通过ISO 2631加权均方根加速度、轮胎-地面接触力变异性和稳定时间评估性能。

Result: 对称阻尼在中等激励下通常足够；非对称阻尼在严苛工况下变得必要；常见的回弹-压缩阻尼比（2~3倍）表现为场景依赖的近优解，而非普适常数。

Conclusion: 该框架为经验性非对称阻尼准则提供了原理性解释，表明其有效性取决于具体激励场景，为悬架设计提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Asymmetric damping is widely used in passive vehicle suspensions, with rebound damping often recommended to exceed compression damping by a factor of two to three. Despite its prevalence, this guideline remains largely empirical and lacks a systematic derivation based on vehicle dynamics and excitation conditions. This paper presents a scenario-driven optimization framework that provides a principled explanation for the effectiveness of asymmetric damping. A minimal quarter-car model is employed to isolate the key mechanisms governing the trade-off between ride comfort, road holding, and transient response, using standardized ISO~8608 road excitations. Rebound and compression damping ratios are treated as independent design variables, and optimal configurations are identified via a stochastic Cross-Entropy algorithm applied to a non-convex, simulation-based objective function. Performance is assessed through ISO~2631 weighted RMS acceleration, tire--ground contact force variability, and settling time. The results show that symmetric damping is often sufficient under moderate excitation, whereas asymmetric damping becomes necessary under severe conditions, with commonly cited rebound-to-compression ratios emerging as scenario-dependent near-optimal solutions rather than universal constants.

</details>


### [268] [A Comparison of Massively Parallel Performance Portable Particle-in-Cell schemes for electrostatic kinetic plasma simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05469)
*Sonali Mayani,Paul Fischill,Sriramkrishnan Muralikrishnan,Andreas Adelmann*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文在静电Vlasov-Poisson系统框架下，通过Landau阻尼算例，系统比较了不同泊松求解器（FFT拟谱、PCG有限差分、有限元）在PIC方法中的性能，以及新型PIF（粒子-傅里叶）方案，并在AMD与Nvidia GPU上验证了可移植性。FFT在绝对时间上最优但适用性受限；PIC中其他求解器时间成本高一个量级但扩展性类似；PIF方案虽成本更高但精度高、可扩展性出色。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在静电Vlasov-Poisson系统的粒子模拟中，泊松求解器的选择直接影响计算效率和可移植性。现有方案在适用性、性能和不同架构间的可移植性方面存在权衡，缺乏系统性的跨架构比较研究。

Method: 基于IPPL库，在512^3和1024^3网格、每网格8粒子的设置下，比较FFT拟谱求解器、矩阵自由有限差分PCG求解器、矩阵自由有限元求解器在PIC循环求解阶段的性能；同时与PIF方案（使用非均匀FFT避免实空间网格）对比。在AMD GPU（LUMI）和Nvidia GPU（Alps、JUWELS Booster）上运行Landau阻尼算例。

Result: FFT求解器在绝对时间上最优，但适用性受限。PIC方案中其他场求解器时间成本高一个数量级，但扩展性与FFT相当。PIF方案作为高保真替代方案，虽比FFT-PIC成本高，但在所有架构上均展现出优异可扩展性。

Conclusion: FFT拟谱求解器在速度上占优但通用性不足；PIC中的PCG和FEM求解器虽慢但扩展性好；PIF方案在精度和可扩展性上表现出色，是高保真模拟的有力候选。

Abstract: We compare different Poisson solvers within the context of an electrostatic Vlasov-Poisson system. These schemes are implemented as part of the IPPL (Independent Parallel Particle Layer) library (Frey et al., 2024), which provides performance portable and dimension independent building blocks for scientific simulations requiring particle-mesh methods, with Eulerian (mesh-based) and Lagrangian (particle-based) approaches. The simulation used to compare the performance and portability of the schemes is Landau damping, part of a set of mini-applications implemented to benchmark and showcase the capabilities of the IPPL library (Muralikrishnan et al., 2024). We use grid-sizes of $512^3$ and $1024^3$ with 8 particles per cell, running with different algorithms in the solve phase of the Particle-in-Cell (PIC) loop: a Fast Fourier Transform (FFT) pseudo-spectral solver, a matrix-free finite difference Preconditioned Conjugate Gradient (PCG) solver, and a matrix-free Finite Element (FEM) solver. We also compare these PIC schemes to the novel Particle-in-Fourier (PIF) scheme, which performs interpolations using non-uniform FFTs thereby avoiding a grid in the real space. We obtain results on different computing architectures, such as AMD GPUs (LUMI at CSC), and Nvidia GPUs (Alps at CSCS and JUWELS Booster at Jülich Supercomputing Center), showcasing portability. In terms of absolute time the FFT solver is advantageous, but is limited in its applicability. All other field solvers in the PIC scheme are an order-of-magnitude more expensive in terms of time, but scale similarly to the FFT case in the electrostatic PIC context. The PIF scheme serves as a high fidelity alternative to standard PIC, and while it is costlier than the FFT-based PIC scheme, it shows excellent scalability on all the architectures.

</details>


### [269] [Duplicate-Aware Shift-and-Lift Carleman Linearization:Structure, Complexity, and Comparative Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05901)
*Takaki Akiba,Youhi Morii*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合移位-提升架构与移动中心展开的Carleman线性化优化方法，通过消除冗余单项式贡献、对称性约化单项式基、紧凑指数键索引和稀疏三元组合并等技术，实现高阶截断的实际计算，并在两个基准测试中验证了方法的收敛性和特定条件下的精度优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Carleman线性化中，随着状态维度和截断阶数的增加，重复的单项式贡献会大量增殖，导致计算开销剧增。现有方法难以高效处理高阶截断带来的局部收敛性和闭合敏感性问题。

Method: 采用移位-提升架构暴露重复指数目标并实现重复感知的系数合并；引入移动中心扩展，使移位和提升围绕演化局部中心联合更新；结合对称性约化单项式基、紧凑指数键索引和稀疏三元组合并技术，降低索引解析开销和写路径不规则性。

Result: 在两个基准（双线性驱动器和逻辑交互）上，两种方法均显示收敛性；所提方法在特定条件下具有精度优势，而非普遍优越性；分析了变量增长、预处理复杂度和截断误差机制。

Conclusion: 移位-提升与移动中心扩展结合的架构能有效处理高阶截断下的冗余问题，但在精度上存在任务依赖性的权衡，而非全面优于Jacobian线性化。

Abstract: The primary objective of this study is to remove duplicated monomial contributions that proliferate in Carleman linearization as state dimension and truncation order increase. To do so, we adopt a shift-and-lift architecture, since it exposes repeated exponent targets and allows duplicate-aware coefficient coalescing during lifted-operator assembly. This architecture also makes high-order truncation practical, but that regime intensifies local convergence and closure sensitivity for higher-order nonlinearities. We therefore pair shift-and-lift with a moving-center expansion so that shift and lift are updated jointly around evolving local centers, improving validity of the truncated model along the trajectory. The resulting workflow combines symmetry-reduced monomial bases, packed exponent-key indexing, and sparse triplet coalescing to preserve truncated affine dynamics while reducing index-resolution overhead and write-path irregularity. We analyze variable growth, preprocessing complexity, and truncation-induced error mechanisms, and we compare against Jacobian linearization through fixed-step error, admissible step size, and cost-at-target-accuracy criteria. Two benchmarks (bilinear driver and logistic interaction) show convergence under refinement for both approaches, with regime-dependent accuracy gains for the proposed method rather than universal superiority.

</details>


### [270] [Quantum Optimization for Electromagnetics: Physics-Informed QAOA for Reconfigurable Intelligent Surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06048)
*Marco Pasquale,Erik M. Åsgrim,Stefano Markidis,Oscar Quevedo-Teruel*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文探讨如何在量子优化中嵌入物理约束（互耦效应），实验表明全局耦合虽能提升波束赋形精度，但在NISQ设备上需采用稀疏距离惩罚模型作为折衷方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子算法优化RIS时忽略互耦等物理约束，导致实际性能严重下降，亟需在量子优化中引入物理信息模型。

Method: 将渐进式物理信息互耦模型嵌入QUBO公式，设计四种Ising相互作用模型（从理想相位模型到全稠密物理模型），在5×5网格上使用QAOA算法进行对比评估。

Result: 全局耦合模型波束赋形精度最高，但密集哈密顿量带来过高路由开销并影响收敛；稀疏距离惩罚模型在精度和硬件可行性间取得平衡。

Conclusion: 物理信息量子优化在数学上可行，但在当前NISQ设备上，稀疏距离惩罚模型是必要的折衷方案。

Abstract: Optimizing Reconfigurable Intelligent Surfaces (RIS) is a high-dimensional combinatorial challenge. Current quantum algorithms often simplify this problem by ignoring physical constraints like mutual coupling, which significantly degrades real-world performance. Rather than targeting a fully realistic RIS description, we embed progressively more physics-informed models of mutual coupling into Quadratic Unconstrained Binary Optimization (QUBO) formulations. We evaluate four Ising interaction models ($J_{ij}$) for the Quantum Approximate Optimization Algorithm (QAOA), ranging from idealized phase-only to fully dense physical models. Analyzing a $5 \times 5$ grid, our results expose a critical trade-off between spatial pointing accuracy and quantum hardware feasibility. While complete global coupling maximizes beamforming precision, dense Hamiltonians introduce prohibitive routing overhead and complicate convergence on near-term processors. Ultimately, we demonstrate that while physics-informed quantum optimization is mathematically viable, sparse, distance-penalized models remain a necessary compromise for execution on current noisy intermediate-scale quantum (NISQ) devices.

</details>
